DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04 AS base
  ARG DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ARG RUST_VERSION=1.88.0
  ARG GO_VERSION=1.20.14
  ARG VERUS_COMMIT=3b6b805ac86cd6640d59468341055c7fa14cff07
  ARG KIND_VERSION=0.23.0
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/anvil
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      build-essential \
      curl \
      git \
      wget \
      software-properties-common \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      libssl-dev \
      pkg-config \
      zlib1g-dev
  # Install Go
  RUN wget https://golang.org/dl/go${GO_VERSION}.linux-amd64.tar.gz && \
      tar -C /usr/local -xzf go${GO_VERSION}.linux-amd64.tar.gz && \
      rm go${GO_VERSION}.linux-amd64.tar.gz
  # Install Rust
  RUN curl https://sh.rustup.rs -sSf | sh -s -- -y --default-toolchain ${RUST_VERSION}
  ENV PATH="/root/.cargo/bin:${PATH}"
  # Install additional Rust tools
  RUN cargo install cargo-watch cargo-verify
  # Install Python dependencies
  RUN pip3 install tabulate
  # Install Z3 SMT solver
  RUN apt-get install -y z3
  # Install Kubernetes tools
  RUN curl -Lo ./kind https://kind.sigs.k8s.io/dl/v${KIND_VERSION}/kind-linux-amd64 && \
      chmod +x ./kind && \
      mv ./kind /usr/local/bin/kind
  RUN curl -LO "https://dl.k8s.io/release/$(curl -L -s https://dl.k8s.io/release/stable.txt)/bin/linux/amd64/kubectl" && \
      chmod +x kubectl && \
      mv kubectl /usr/local/bin/
  # Clone and build Verus
  RUN git clone https://github.com/verus-lang/verus.git && \
      cd verus && \
      git checkout ${VERUS_COMMIT} && \
      cargo build --release
  # Set environment paths
  ENV PATH="/usr/local/go/bin:${PATH}"
  ENV RUST_HOME="/root/.cargo"
  ENV VERUS_HOME="/home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/anvil/verus"
  # Cleanup
  RUN apt-get clean && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  WORKDIR /home/cc/EnvGym/data-gpt-4.1mini/anvil
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04 AS base
  ARG DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ARG RUST_VERSION=1.88.0
  ARG GO_VERSION=1.20.14
  ARG VERUS_COMMIT=3b6b805ac86cd6640d59468341055c7fa14cff07
  ARG KIND_VERSION=0.23.0
  WORKDIR /anvil
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      build-essential \
      curl \
      git \
      wget \
      software-properties-common \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      libssl-dev \
      pkg-config \
      zlib1g-dev \
      ca-certificates
  # Install Go
  RUN wget https://golang.org/dl/go${GO_VERSION}.linux-amd64.tar.gz && \
      tar -C /usr/local -xzf go${GO_VERSION}.linux-amd64.tar.gz && \
      rm go${GO_VERSION}.linux-amd64.tar.gz
  # Install Rust
  RUN curl https://sh.rustup.rs -sSf | sh -s -- -y --default-toolchain ${RUST_VERSION}
  ENV PATH="/root/.cargo/bin:${PATH}"
  # Install additional Rust tools
  RUN cargo install cargo-watch cargo-verify
  # Install Python dependencies
  RUN pip3 install tabulate
  # Install Z3 SMT solver
  RUN apt-get install -y z3
  # Install Kubernetes tools
  RUN curl -Lo ./kind https://kind.sigs.k8s.io/dl/v${KIND_VERSION}/kind-linux-amd64 && \
      chmod +x ./kind && \
      mv ./kind /usr/local/bin/kind
  RUN curl -LO "https://dl.k8s.io/release/$(curl -L -s https://dl.k8s.io/release/stable.txt)/bin/linux/amd64/kubectl" && \
      chmod +x kubectl && \
      mv kubectl /usr/local/bin/
  # Clone and build Verus with retry mechanism
  RUN mkdir -p /anvil/verus && \
      cd /anvil/verus && \
      git clone --depth 1 --branch main https://github.com/verus-lang/verus.git . || \
      (sleep 5 && git clone --depth 1 --branch main https://github.com/verus-lang/verus.git .) && \
      git checkout ${VERUS_COMMIT} && \
      cargo build --release --verbose || cargo build --release
  # Set environment paths
  ENV PATH="/usr/local/go/bin:${PATH}"
  ENV RUST_HOME="/root/.cargo"
  ENV VERUS_HOME="/anvil/verus"
  # Cleanup
  RUN apt-get clean && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  WORKDIR /anvil
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04 AS base
  ARG DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ARG RUST_VERSION=1.88.0
  ARG GO_VERSION=1.20.14
  ARG VERUS_COMMIT=3b6b805ac86cd6640d59468341055c7fa14cff07
  ARG KIND_VERSION=0.23.0
  WORKDIR /anvil
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      build-essential \
      curl \
      git \
      wget \
      software-properties-common \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      libssl-dev \
      pkg-config \
      zlib1g-dev \
      ca-certificates
  # Install Go
  RUN wget https://golang.org/dl/go${GO_VERSION}.linux-amd64.tar.gz && \
      tar -C /usr/local -xzf go${GO_VERSION}.linux-amd64.tar.gz && \
      rm go${GO_VERSION}.linux-amd64.tar.gz
  # Install Rust
  RUN curl https://sh.rustup.rs -sSf | sh -s -- -y --default-toolchain ${RUST_VERSION}
  ENV PATH="/root/.cargo/bin:${PATH}"
  # Install additional Rust tools
  RUN cargo install cargo-watch cargo-verify
  # Install Python dependencies
  RUN pip3 install tabulate
  # Install Z3 SMT solver
  RUN apt-get install -y z3
  # Install Kubernetes tools
  RUN curl -Lo ./kind https://kind.sigs.k8s.io/dl/v${KIND_VERSION}/kind-linux-amd64 && \
      chmod +x ./kind && \
      mv ./kind /usr/local/bin/kind
  RUN curl -LO "https://dl.k8s.io/release/$(curl -L -s https://dl.k8s.io/release/stable.txt)/bin/linux/amd64/kubectl" && \
      chmod +x kubectl && \
      mv kubectl /usr/local/bin/
  # Clone and build Verus with enhanced error handling
  RUN mkdir -p /anvil/verus && \
      cd /anvil/verus && \
      git clone --recursive https://github.com/verus-lang/verus.git . && \
      git fetch origin ${VERUS_COMMIT} && \
      git checkout ${VERUS_COMMIT} && \
      cargo build --release
  # Set environment paths
  ENV PATH="/usr/local/go/bin:${PATH}"
  ENV RUST_HOME="/root/.cargo"
  ENV VERUS_HOME="/anvil/verus"
  # Clone the Anvil repository
  RUN git clone https://github.com/microsoft/anvil.git /anvil/repository
  # Cleanup
  RUN apt-get clean && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  WORKDIR /anvil/repository
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 3 ---

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04 AS base
  ARG DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ARG RUST_VERSION=1.88.0
  ARG GO_VERSION=1.20.14
  ARG VERUS_COMMIT=3b6b805ac86cd6640d59468341055c7fa14cff07
  ARG KIND_VERSION=0.23.0
  WORKDIR /anvil
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      build-essential \
      curl \
      git \
      wget \
      software-properties-common \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      libssl-dev \
      pkg-config \
      zlib1g-dev \
      ca-certificates
  # Install Go
  RUN wget https://golang.org/dl/go${GO_VERSION}.linux-amd64.tar.gz && \
      tar -C /usr/local -xzf go${GO_VERSION}.linux-amd64.tar.gz && \
      rm go${GO_VERSION}.linux-amd64.tar.gz
  # Install Rust
  RUN curl https://sh.rustup.rs -sSf | sh -s -- -y --default-toolchain ${RUST_VERSION}
  ENV PATH="/root/.cargo/bin:${PATH}"
  # Install additional Rust tools
  RUN cargo install cargo-watch cargo-verify
  # Install Python dependencies
  RUN pip3 install tabulate
  # Install Z3 SMT solver
  RUN apt-get install -y z3
  # Install Kubernetes tools
  RUN curl -Lo ./kind https://kind.sigs.k8s.io/dl/v${KIND_VERSION}/kind-linux-amd64 && \
      chmod +x ./kind && \
      mv ./kind /usr/local/bin/kind
  RUN curl -LO "https://dl.k8s.io/release/$(curl -L -s https://dl.k8s.io/release/stable.txt)/bin/linux/amd64/kubectl" && \
      chmod +x kubectl && \
      mv kubectl /usr/local/bin/
  # Clone and build Verus with detailed error handling
  RUN mkdir -p /anvil/verus && \
      cd /anvil/verus && \
      git clone https://github.com/verus-lang/verus.git . || (echo "Git clone failed" && exit 1) && \
      git fetch origin ${VERUS_COMMIT} || (echo "Git fetch failed" && exit 1) && \
      git checkout ${VERUS_COMMIT} || (echo "Git checkout failed" && exit 1) && \
      cargo build --release || (echo "Cargo build failed" && exit 1)
  # Set environment paths
  ENV PATH="/usr/local/go/bin:${PATH}"
  ENV RUST_HOME="/root/.cargo"
  ENV VERUS_HOME="/anvil/verus"
  # Clone the Anvil repository
  RUN git clone https://github.com/microsoft/anvil.git /anvil/repository
  # Cleanup
  RUN apt-get clean && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  WORKDIR /anvil/repository
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]

  FROM ubuntu:22.04 AS base
  ARG DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ARG RUST_VERSION=1.88.0
  ARG GO_VERSION=1.20.14
  ARG VERUS_COMMIT=3b6b805ac86cd6640d59468341055c7fa14cff07
  ARG KIND_VERSION=0.23.0
  WORKDIR /anvil
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      build-essential \
      curl \
      git \
      wget \
      software-properties-common \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      libssl-dev \
      pkg-config \
      zlib1g-dev \
      ca-certificates \
      && apt-get clean \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install Go
  RUN wget https://golang.org/dl/go${GO_VERSION}.linux-amd64.tar.gz && \
      tar -C /usr/local -xzf go${GO_VERSION}.linux-amd64.tar.gz && \
      rm go${GO_VERSION}.linux-amd64.tar.gz
  # Install Rust
  RUN curl https://sh.rustup.rs -sSf | sh -s -- -y --default-toolchain ${RUST_VERSION}
  ENV PATH="/root/.cargo/bin:${PATH}"
  # Install additional Rust tools
  RUN cargo install cargo-watch cargo-verify
  # Install Python dependencies
  RUN pip3 install tabulate
  # Install Z3 SMT solver
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y z3 \
      && apt-get clean \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install Kubernetes tools
  RUN curl -Lo ./kind https://kind.sigs.k8s.io/dl/v${KIND_VERSION}/kind-linux-amd64 && \
      chmod +x ./kind && \
      mv ./kind /usr/local/bin/kind
  RUN curl -LO "https://dl.k8s.io/release/$(curl -L -s https://dl.k8s.io/release/stable.txt)/bin/linux/amd64/kubectl" && \
      chmod +x kubectl && \
      mv kubectl /usr/local/bin/
  # Clone and build Verus with improved error handling
  RUN mkdir -p /anvil/verus && \
      cd /anvil/verus && \
      git clone https://github.com/verus-lang/verus.git . 2>&1 | tee git_clone.log && \
      git fetch origin ${VERUS_COMMIT} 2>&1 | tee git_fetch.log && \
      git checkout ${VERUS_COMMIT} 2>&1 | tee git_checkout.log && \
      cargo build --release 2>&1 | tee cargo_build.log
  # Set environment paths
  ENV PATH="/usr/local/go/bin:${PATH}"
  ENV RUST_HOME="/root/.cargo"
  ENV VERUS_HOME="/anvil/verus"
  # Clone the Anvil repository
  RUN git clone https://github.com/microsoft/anvil.git /anvil/repository
  WORKDIR /anvil/repository
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
--- End of Iteration 6 ---

DOCKERFILE:
  FROM ubuntu:22.04 AS base
  ARG DEBIAN_FRONTEND=noninteractive
  ARG RUST_VERSION=1.88.0
  ARG GO_VERSION=1.20.14
  ARG VERUS_COMMIT=3b6b805ac86cd6640d59468341055c7fa14cff07
  ARG KIND_VERSION=0.23.0
  WORKDIR /anvil
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y \
      build-essential \
      curl \
      git \
      wget \
      software-properties-common \
      python3 \
      python3-pip \
      libssl-dev \
      pkg-config \
      zlib1g-dev \
      ca-certificates \
      && apt-get clean \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install Go
  RUN wget https://golang.org/dl/go${GO_VERSION}.linux-amd64.tar.gz && \
      tar -C /usr/local -xzf go${GO_VERSION}.linux-amd64.tar.gz && \
      rm go${GO_VERSION}.linux-amd64.tar.gz
  # Install Rust
  RUN curl https://sh.rustup.rs -sSf | sh -s -- -y --default-toolchain ${RUST_VERSION}
  ENV PATH="/root/.cargo/bin:${PATH}"
  # Install additional Rust tools
  RUN cargo install cargo-watch cargo-verify
  # Install Python dependencies
  RUN pip3 install tabulate
  # Install Z3 SMT solver
  RUN apt-get update && apt-get install -y z3 \
      && apt-get clean \
      && rm -rf /var/lib/apt/lists/*
  # Install Kubernetes tools
  RUN curl -Lo ./kind https://kind.sigs.k8s.io/dl/v${KIND_VERSION}/kind-linux-amd64 && \
      chmod +x ./kind && \
      mv ./kind /usr/local/bin/kind
  RUN curl -LO "https://dl.k8s.io/release/$(curl -L -s https://dl.k8s.io/release/stable.txt)/bin/linux/amd64/kubectl" && \
      chmod +x kubectl && \
      mv kubectl /usr/local/bin/
  # Clone and build Verus with improved error handling
  RUN mkdir -p /anvil/verus && \
      cd /anvil/verus && \
      git clone https://github.com/verus-lang/verus.git . 2>&1 | tee git_clone.log && \
      git fetch origin ${VERUS_COMMIT} 2>&1 | tee git_fetch.log && \
      git checkout ${VERUS_COMMIT} 2>&1 | tee git_checkout.log && \
      cargo build --release 2>&1 | tee cargo_build.log
  # Set environment paths
  ENV PATH="/usr/local/go/bin:${PATH}"
  ENV RUST_HOME="/root/.cargo"
  ENV VERUS_HOME="/anvil/verus"
  # Clone the Anvil repository with retry and verbose logging
  RUN mkdir -p /anvil/repository && \
      cd /anvil/repository && \
      (for i in 1 2 3; do \
          git clone https://github.com/microsoft/anvil.git . && break || \
          echo "Clone attempt $i failed, retrying..." && \
          sleep 5; \
      done) 2>&1 | tee git_clone_log.txt
  WORKDIR /anvil/repository
  CMD ["/bin/bash"]
